searchForms = $('form[action=\"/search\"]').css('position', 'relative').each(function() {\n    // Grabbing text input.\n    var input = $(this).find('input[name=\"show_q\"]');\n    // Adding a list for showing search results.\n    var offSet = input.position().top + input.innerHeight();\n    $('<ul class=\"search-results z-depth-1\"></ul>').css( { 'position': 'absolute', 'left': '0px', 'top': offSet } ).appendTo($(this)).hide();\n    // Listening to keyup and change on the text field within these search forms.\n    input.attr('autocomplete', 'off').on('keyup change', function() {\n      // What's the search term?\n      var term = $(this).val();\n      // What's the search form?\n      var form = $(this).closest('form');\n      // What's the search URL?\n      var searchURL = '/search?type=product&q=*+' + term + '+*'+'+tag:searchable';\n      // What's the search results list?\n      var resultsList = form.find('.search-results');\n      // If that's a new term and it contains at least 3 characters.\n      if (term.length > 0 && term != $(this).attr('data-old-term')) {\n        // Saving old query.\n        $(this).attr('data-old-term', term);\n        // Killing any Ajax request that's currently being processed.\n        if (currentAjaxRequest != null) currentAjaxRequest.abort();\n        // Pulling results.\n        currentAjaxRequest = $.getJSON(searchURL + '&view=json', function(data) {\n          // Reset results.\n          resultsList.empty();\n          // If we have no results.\n          if (data.results_count == 0) {\n            $('#evo-searchform-submit').prop('disabled', true);\n            resultsList.html('<li><span class=\"title no-result\">Search No Result</span></li>');\n            resultsList.fadeIn(200);\n            if (term.length == 0) {\n              resultsList.hide();\n            }\n          } else {\n            $('#evo-searchform-submit').prop('disabled', false);\n            // If we have results.\n            $.each(data.results, function(index, item) {\n              if (index > 6) {\n                return;\n              }\n\n              var link = $('<a></a>').attr('href', item.url);\n              link.append('<span class=\"thumbnail col s3 m3\"><img src=\"' + item.thumbnail + '\" /></span>');\n              link.append('<span class=\"title col s9 m9\">' + item.title + '</span>');\n              link.wrap('<li class=\"row\"></li>');\n              resultsList.append(link.parent());\n            });\n            // The Ajax request will return at the most 10 results.\n            // If there are more than 10, let's link to the search results page.\n            if(data.results_count > 0) {\n              // resultsList.append('<li><span class=\"title\"><a href=\"' + searchURL + '\">See all results (' + data.results_count + ')</a></span></li>');\n              resultsList.append('<li><span class=\"title see-all-result\"><a href=\"' + searchURL + '\">See All Results </a></span></li>');\n            }\n            resultsList.fadeIn(200);\n          }\n        });\n      }\n    });\n  });\n  // Clicking outside makes the results disappear.\n  $('body').bind('click', function(){\n    $('.search-results').hide();\n  });\n});\n</script>\n\n<!-- Some styles to get you started. -->\n<style>\n.search-results {\n  z-index: 8889;\n ($('#cart-items li').length <= 3) {\n      $('.cart-item-arrow').css('display', 'none');\n    }\n  }\n\n  //取cookies函数\n  function getCookie(name) {\n    var arr = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(\"(^| )\"+name+\"=([^;]*)(;|$)\"));\n    if(arr != null) return unescape(arr[2]); return null;\n  }\n\n</script>\n\n        \n      </li>\n    </ul>\n    <div class=\"mobile-navbar\">\n
